The nose behind this fragrance is Rodrigo Flores-Roux. Top notes are Clementine, Lemon, Mandarin Orange, Bergamot, Thyme and Marjoram; middle notes are Petitgrain and Ginger; base notes are Woody Notes, Musk, Orris Root and Amber. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>The house of John Varvatos presents its new masculine fragrance Artisan Pure in Fall of 2017 as a limited edition of the original Artisan from 2009.</p>

<p>"John Varvatos Artisan Pure is a crisp, woody, citrus scent inspired by the lush hills of Xalapa, Mexico and its vast coffee and citrus groves. Now available for purchase, the first 100 bottles will be personally signed by John Varvatos."</p>

<p>The fragrance is announced as a sharp, woody and citrusy, described as refined as it is cool. The composition highlights three different aspects of petitgrain: it leaves, branches and fruits.</p>

<p>Top notes: lemon, bergamot, mandarin, clementine, thyme, marjoram<br />
Heart: petitgrain, ginger<br />
Base: woods, orris root, amber, musk</p>

<p>The face of the campaign is American actor and model Daniel Henney. The fragrance is available as a 75 and 125 ml of Eau de Toilette.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a     <div class="strike-title"><span>All Reviews By Date</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2332141" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2332141" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="fanumwiththecannon"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2030404"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="fanumwiththecannon" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2332141ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2332141" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2030404">fanumwiththecannon</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-29">10/29/24 23:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Picture yourself standing by a slow-moving river surrounded by lush greenery, right after a light summer rain. The ground is damp, releasing a soft, earthy aroma that mingles with the dewy freshness of orange blossoms and sweet mandarin in the air. A gentle breeze stirs, bringing with it the scent of ripe lemon trees and hints of delicate herbs growing nearby. The air feels light and clean, with a grounding warmth that comes from woody notes lingering in the background.<br />
<br />
John Varvatos Artisan Pure captures this serene, refreshing moment in nature—crisp, citrusy, and effortlessly natural.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2332141"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2332141#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2328097" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2328097" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SiddhantSuryawanshi"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1690312"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1690312.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SiddhantSuryawanshi" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2328097ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2328097" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1690312">SiddhantSuryawanshi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-26">10/26/24 05:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Artisan Pure's citrus quartet (limonene, citral, citronellal) is actually a paragon of balance. But your brain's reward centers were being bombarded with heavy hitters in 2017. Everyone was chasing oud and ambroxan dopamine hits, and thus this clean composition just didn't hack the limbic system hard enough.<br />
<br />
The 'Too Clean' Trap: Those beautiful citrus molecules are volatile; they peace out in 30-60 mins. The clean musks don't manipulate your primitive brain like animalics do. No addictive molecules (missing that ambroxan/vanilla one-two punch that makes modern frags so habit-forming). It's molecularly elegant but doesn't play dirty with your neurons.<br />
<br />
Evolution really did this frag dirty. Our primal brains are wired to remember danger signals (animalics), food signals (gourmands), and mate-attraction signals (heavy musks). Pure's clean profile doesn't trigger these survival circuits. Same as bringing poetry to a knife fight; beautiful but not threatening enough to remember.<br />
<br />
The Marketing Psychology sealed its fate: No controversy = no neural imprint. Didn't spark enough amygdala activity to create strong memory traces. Your brain filed it under 'safe but forgettable'. They crafted something pristine when the market wanted psychological warfare. Sometimes molecular elegance isn't enough - you need to hack some neurons!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2328097"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2328097#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2322191" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/939475">caifan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-06">08/06/24 14:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Artisan Pure is a citrus, herbal and musky fragrance.<br />
<br />
Its opening is fresh, sparkling and citrusy, slightly synthetic, which quickly transitions to a citrusy, spicy herbal sensation that is very pleasant and easy to wear. Once it reaches its drying phase, a musky and woody base is perceived, but the citrus always remains.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is undoubtedly for daytime use, in hot seasons like spring and summer, I like it to start the day with energy and that feeling of cheerful freshness.<br />
<br />
Its longevity wasn't bad at all, I expected it to last less, but at least it stayed with me for almost 8 hours. and its aromatic sillage is a little strange, because sometimes it seems like it has already disappeared and suddenly I get bursts of the smell.<br />
<br />
I bought a travel version that is 17 ml, for now I will continue using it, then I will think about whether to buy a larger bottle, for now I will enjoy it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2205264">Picky_snout</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-03">08/03/24 17:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I’m a huge fan of the John Varvatos house. I live in Southern California and the brand just vibes here. So when I saw this interesting looking bottle of artisan pure for $40 on fragnet, I thought, hell, it’s JV, I’ll blind buy a bottle. Ohhh boy….<br />
<br />
If I had smelled this at macys I would have immediately passed on this, not even giving a thought to sprits it on my skin to see how it settles. The citrus notes bitch slaps like Rick James in the 80’s. I could not get over it. But I had a whole bottle…fug it, let’s wear this, it’s 105° out, at least this is light. This is where this frag took a turn<br />
<br />
After about 10 minutes, the top notes faded and what was left was this dry, musky, beach sandy scent that was so goddamn enjoyable, I went straight to the store to buy steak cause the scent got me into a pool party mood. I doused myself, sat next to the water and enjoyed the scent of my carne asada grilling and me smelling like summer vacation. <br />
<br />
What I thought was a huge mistake on my first blind buy is truly becoming my “go-to” or my “relax at home” or “can’t decide” fragrance of my collection. At least for summer especially during these heat waves.<br />
<br />
This is the best fragrance purchase I’ve ever made, not because this scent is particularly amazing, but because I learned to change my expectations and first impressions of other fragrances. I learned to always buy decants from now on, you just have to wear fragrances for a day or 2 to really gauge the time, place, etc of what colognes can really bring. I have grown to absolutely love this scent, not just because of the way it smells, but because of the mood it puts me in.<br />
<br />
Edit: experimented with my first layering, this slaps with D&amp;G light blue, 4:1 ratio because Light blue is strong.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2238076"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2238076#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2236625" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I love the scent of lemon/lime leaves close to your nose, and to me that is what best describes it. <br />
In terms of notes, it does not give that mandarine/tangerine aroma. Instead, is a general citrus, leaning lemon. It has that profile of wood-lemon baby cologne they use to put on us in the eighties. If you are open to get reacquainted with a smoother version of said note, you might discover quite a pleasant scent.<br />
It doesn't last long, though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2213569"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2213569#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209798" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I honestly expected a generic, male scent like a head and shoulders shampoo. I expected nothing, and instead was met with everything I love in a fresh citrus perfume.<br />
<br />
To me, it's citrus blended with woodiness. Bitter citrus peels, mainly a fresh, juicy, lemon. Not sharp or burning and does not remind of cleaning products.  The blast of citrus is strong until it settles in a few minutes and the woody base and herbs become a more prominent. I honestly smell aromatic vetiver and just a little bit of thyme.<br />
<br />
It's unisex in my opinion, fresh, aromatic goodness for everyone. Office friendly for sure. However, the silage could be a problem, it's the only thing making be hesitate to buy a full bottle. It's a skin scent basically. It does last for hours but it does not project. I will buy a bottle when I become rich enough lol.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2187963"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2187963#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2187900" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Deep, juicy citrus with calming and aromatic greens &amp; woods. One thing this immediately reminded me of is CK One, as it gives off a green tea refreshing vibe, but much more modern and clean. There isn't too much to say about this one, it's nothing extraordinary, but man is it good. An instant mood lifter. As others mentioned, there is a bit of a "fruit loops" note in here (akin to something like the fruitiness of Cedrat Boise), but as weird as it sounds it works so well. I sampled it before buying a bottle, and I didn't even make the connection at first until reading the reviews after. So if smelling like cereal is a concern, don't worry about it. It's impossible to not like this one. Performance isn't stellar but it's not horrible, it gets the job done.<br />
<br />
Bonus points for having one of the most aesthetic bottles in my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2181527"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2181527#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2169031" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1288074">danomar13</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-21">05/21/24 05:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>First thing I would like to mention is the atomizer on this bottle is abysmal. Clone houses like armaf and lataffa have better atomizers and are cheaper. I understand this fragrance is not that expensive but still.. it costs them nominal amounts of money to just get a better one. <br />
<br />
The actual juice inside the bottle is quite good for a freshie. The opening is a pleasant, clean, round lemony citrus scent and a backdrop of a herbal undertone. Nothing groundbreaking or anything but quite enjoyable. In my opinion the fragrance has performance issues in the early spring and shines best during those hot days. That being said, carrying a decant of the stuff will do you just fine. On my skin, it projects for 2-3 hours on my body then becomes a skin scent after 4-5. On hotter days it projects about 1 hour longer. As with all things, the performance depends with your skin type. I personally enjoy wearing it around the house or if I am at work as its non-intrusive. <br />
<br />
To date, it is my favorite John Varvatos fragrance because of its simplicity. I would recommend giving it a try (specially since summer is around the corner).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2162956"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2162956#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2160658" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2148943" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Sanguine_scenttrails"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1831365"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1831365.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Sanguine_scenttrails" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Ombre-Leather-2018-50239.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.50239.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ombré Leather (2018)"title="Ombré Leather (2018)"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2148943ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2148943" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1831365">Sanguine_scenttrails</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-07">05/07/24 19:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Artisan Pure sits strangely (and beautifully) between natural and synthetic. It is the smell of looking out at the natural beauty of the tropics... from the comfort of your Five Star hotel balcony. The word that keeps coming to mind is "Resort". Artisan Pure smells beachy, affluent, attractive, and fresh. The epitome of resort wear in a masculine leaning fragrance.<br />
<br />
To be honest I don't get much neroli in here, but what I do smell is a sexy aromatic citrus cologne. This is Pedro Pascal in a white linen shirt at the Westin. Notes wise, we have a fresh citrus fragrance with heavy ambroxan/woods in the base. The star of this is an INCREDIBLE ginger note that never gets too spicy, but gives a sexy edge similar to the ginger magic in L'homme by YSL. Whatever neroli may be here rounds everything out and uplifts for summer. <br />
<br />
I simply have no idea what people are talking about longevity wise. This outperforms any citrus frag I own by a longshot- I easily got 8 hours from this. I wouldn't say this is similar at all to TF Neroli Portofino, etc. But the neroli in this pulls it into a DNA that would be enjoyed by fans of the aforementioned. Layers great with 4711, and I like it a lot- but ultimately will stick with a more neroli forward naturalistic fragrance for summer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2148943"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2148943#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2147068" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2147068" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Isomies"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1182455"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1182455.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Isomies" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Santa-Maria-Novella/Vetiver-11459.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.11459.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Vetiver"title="Vetiver"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2147068ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2147068" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1182455">Isomies</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-05">05/05/24 23:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Most "hidden" nature "citrus summer frag" for shure! It's the mix of summers in the north and Mediterranean costs. Not forgetting the New Hampton east cost of Usa. The balance is phenomenal as almost all Varvatos creations. For longevity I've suggest to all who it might concern, pls. do as follows; first layer a neutral mix (1:1) of attar oil and perfume alcohol. Attar oil should be floral or light smell. Then layer/spray a destinated fragrance on that. On that way you'll get extra longevity (fixative) to your decided original fragrance. This method will combine all notes, top, middle and bases as a "hole".</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2147068"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2147068#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2144262" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; After a quarter the citric sourness emerges and the herbs diminish. Its projection shrinking, and its personality muted.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2106009">Gabrielepresta</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-03">05/03/24 05:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>➡️ "ARTISANE PURE'' by John Varvatos<br />
<br />
 Concentration: Eau de Toilette<br />
 Trend: Unisex<br />
 Seasons: Spring/Summer<br />
 Occasions: Summer lunches/dinners, hot days<br />
 Average cost<br />
<br />
 It's the turn of a brand unknown to most, but which has certainly been able to stand out in the art of perfumery for the excellent overall quality of its products.<br />
 Here we are faced first of all with a bottle that, just by looking at it, would be a good gift to make a great impression on anyone.  Yet it is in its first sprays that the real value of this wonder is definitively understood.<br />
 A mixed-citrus smell that is strong at first but delicate over time;  as intimate as it is majestic for those within conversational distance.  A fresh, clean, so simple and really lovely.<br />
 Unisex and therefore also suitable for women who do not only appreciate the extremely sweet or the floral, a shame only for a duration which, as with almost all medium-high temperature fragrances, is the most criticizable characteristic.<br />
 Go out for a walk in the middle of June with a linen shirt and this perfume on, and you will never want to go home again.  Guaranteed.<br />
<br />
 Bottle: 10/10 ✅<br />
 Projection: 7/10 ✅<br />
 Duration:6/10 ✅<br />
 Fragrance: 9/10 ✅<br />
<br />
 Final rating: 8.5/10 ✅<br />
<br />

I have to be careful where I wear this juice because I don't always want to smell that sexy in a professional setting, rather just clean. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2114794" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="docelder"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1924816"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="docelder" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2114794ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2114794" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1924816">docelder</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-05">04/05/24 00:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The best Varvatos fragrance IMO. It's a summer scent, or year round in South Florida or anywhere with high heat and high humidity conditions. As others have said, I also wish this one was a little bit stronger and a little longer lasting and yet, if it was then it really wouldn't be an any day Summer scent. The citrus top on this is exceptional and the herbaceous element gives a comfort type vibe. In all, it's beautifully put together and you will wish it were stronger in part, because it just smells really nice and you don't want it to end. If it was a little stronger, it could be put into a niche bottle. But then, it wouldn't be a practical Summer scent, but niche fragrances don't face those same practical restraints that designers face. In all practicality, who needs another niche strength scent anyway, that smells really great but can't be worn to work, or to the airport, or to the movies? This has arms length projection with 4 sprays for 2 to 3 hours and becomes an up close scent for 6 hours, with a pleasant skin scent after. This is well worth the price it is going for currently. Look at it in the same way as any other of the well blended male citrus top fragrances and the performance makes perfect sense. It would make a great wear to work scent, where you don't want to be noticed across a cubicle or a conference table. Or, it would be a great scent to apply just for going out to dinner. It is what it is. It does what it does extremely well. Just saw a 4.2 oz tester at Joma for $30 and picked up a backup. It came in a retail looking box with just a tester sticker on the outside box. Has the cap and all. On that note, the atomizer on my original bottle is suboptimal. I speculated part of the performance issue is that atomizer as it does not disperse the scent well. I have recently acquired a backup bottle. Well, I swapped the atomizer top from the new one to the one I have been using, and it's significantly better. I would say adequate. I do believe the longevity itself is improved just as a result of this swap alone.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2114794"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2114794#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2113705" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I wish the performance was better.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2061210"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2061210#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2058265" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2058265" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="waymonbrown84"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1421242"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="waymonbrown84" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Burberry/London-for-Men-804.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.804.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="London for Men"title="London for Men"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2058265ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2058265" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1421242">waymonbrown84</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-10">02/10/24 12:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've been wearing this for a few years now and have went through sizes 2.5 - 4.2 in a few bottles. It simply smells great. <br />
<br />
You're going to get a crisp, orangey, bergamot, citrus affair with some herbs that don't smell like the kitchen or medicines but used for their added depth and spicy effects vs using actual spices. Green-citrus, crisp, almost mouthwatering, soft woody, intelligent use of musk is what you'll get. <br />
<br />
The original Artisan conjures up thoughts of being at a business luncheon with a cool blazer and slacks but not a suit and you'd smell like the most trustworthy guy in the room. The OG Artisan is like brunch in a bottle, reminsicent of TF Neroli Portonfino in vibe and in many ways in scent. OG Artisan even has a wicker basket like feel to just like the bottles design. I attribute that to the herbs in Artisan. Artisan Pure cleans things up a bit with using herbs for their facets instead of the scent being an all out herbal citrus like the original. Artisan Pure is the even easier to get along with brother of Artisan and you invite him to hang out with your crew more often to shoot pool and hit up a bar just because he's a cool guy. Maybe a little less personality than big bro but that's perfectly fine as blends in even easier as just being a really cool dude- that is his personality edge. <br />
<br />
I like both but Artisan Pure is just the sort of scent that is undeniable to keep coming back to even when I think I can move on to other citrus scents. It's more masculine than Dior Homme Cologne,  without that grey steely musk and is far less money online. You can use 10 sprays if you wanted and you'll still be completely fine. It comes off as being a little week to your nose until you get used to how it performs. If I go 6 sprays on my neck I know it'll be there 6-8 hrs later. <br />
<br />
It's quality and could easily be a $75 scent in the 4.2 oz at stores with no discounted online option and it would be worth it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2002371" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheDogfatherHTX"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1824841.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheDogfatherHTX" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Givenchy/Gentleman-Eau-de-Parfum-Reserve-Privee-71272.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.71272.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gentleman Eau de Parfum Reserve Privée"title="Gentleman Eau de Parfum Reserve Privée"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2002371ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2002371" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841">TheDogfatherHTX</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-15">12/15/23 21:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is one of the most hyped John Varvatos fragrances in the community. Several YouTubers have featured this fragrance in some of their Top 10 lists. I gave into the hype and blind bought it. Read on to find out how that went;<br />
<br />
Scent:<br />
Opening is citrusy, green, and spicy. The primary notes I get are clementine/mandarin orange, petitgrain, lemon, thyme, and ginger. The strongest of these notes are the clementine/mandarin, petitgrain, and lemon that give it a sweet, sour, and juicy fruit scent with a strong green quality. This is followed by the thyme and ginger that add to the green qualities and give a spicy kick in the background. The clementine note in this fragrance is very realistic and is reminiscent of cutting open a fresh Halo Orange. The dry down is citrusy, woody, and musky. The primary notes I get are lemon, wood, and musk. The strongest of these notes are the lemon and musk for a citrusy, clean freshness. This is followed by the wood note for a sturdy and woody background. There's also just a bit of the green notes left, barely noticeable.<br />
<br />
Performance:<br />
Initial projection is strong at around 6 feet. Sillage is strong as well with an easily noticeable scent trail. After about 3-4 hours the projection was about arms length and there was still an easily noticeable scent trail. At the 6 hour mark the projection was within 12 inches and the scent trail was slightly noticeable. Barely there, but still there. The fragrance became a skin scent soon thereafter.<br />
<br />
When to wear:<br />
This is a pure spring/summer scent most suitable for daytime wear. Typically I would say a fresh scent like this would be suitable for the office, but there's something about this one that makes me say otherwise. I can't quite put my finger on it. In any case, it's a great choice for going out in the sun.<br />
<br />
Blind buy:<br />
If you like fresh and citrusy summer scents but can also appreciate unique twists on them, this is a safe blind buy for you.<br />
<br />
Final verdict:<br />
I can understand the hype for this fragrance. It's your typical citrusy, fresh, and clean summer fragrance; but made interesting with an pleasant twist. The scent is really nice, the performance is respectable, and it's unique enough to stand out in a crowd. I'm glad that I have this in my collection for something a little different during the summer, and at a price point of around $30 for 125ml this is a steal. Scoop this one up on your next fragrance haul and thank me later.<br />
<br />
Scent: 8/10<br />
Longevity: 6/10<br />
Sillage: 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="2002371"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=2002371#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2000659" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1996777" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EmJay87"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1587468"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1587468.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EmJay87" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/724-75754.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.75754.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="724"title="724"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1996777ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1996777" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1587468">EmJay87</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-09">12/09/23 09:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Quite a bitter orange/mandarin, so not a sweet citrus. Nice though. The bitter opening also has a herbal quality to it so that also keeps it from being "sweet". Because of that it is just as much a spring scent as it is a summer one. Daytime. Casual. Not very complex - what you smell at first is pretty much what you get, but for a few hours it does a decent job. The herbal opening eventually settles and you get a bitter citrus scent for the rest of the wear. <br />
<br />
Moderate-to-close sillage and projection, and in terms of longevity I got about 3 solid hours in a full wearing when testing it (on skin). Not very long-lasting at all, but if you can find a situation for it (gym, short errands etc.) it's OK. The one caveat I would add to the longevity is that I am wearing this in colder weather currently (indoors). I know weather affects longevity and performance, especially in citrus/lighter fragrances, but it doesn't feel like a scent you spray at the start of a workday and get faint hints of on the way home, unless you oversprayed.<br />
<br />
If you can pick it up for cheap or sample it, I'd say try it. But the longevity isn't good enough for this to be your go-to spring/summer workhorse. <br />
<br />
Blind by safe, as long as you're OK with your citruses being closer to the bitter end of the spectrum than sweet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1996777"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1996777#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1989048" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1648729"><a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="0c5b616d7e3a3a3b3f4c6b616d6560226f6361">[email&#160;protected]</a></b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-22">09/22/23 07:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There aren’t many summer fragrances you can buy that have this level of sophistication. Sweet balsamic tartness with the opening that lingers well into the dry down. Bitter orange and a really interesting green pepper backbone are the framework. That herbaceous green pepper is what separates this fragrance from many, many others others. It smell mature but playful and I think any age could pull this off. If you are younger this will project some sophistication and maturity and if you are older it will project a playful, energetic vibe. Great fragrance. Kind of one and done summer choice for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1934484"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1934484#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1934203" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1797683">JoshSmells</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-21">09/21/23 23:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A steal for the price. It definitely does its own thing while still being fairly mass appealing. Citrus, spices, ginger, florals, woods, some sweetness with a slight beachy vibe. Evolves beautifully on the skin. Not something I'm always in the mood for but a great fragrance nonetheless.<br />
<br />
I really loved the original Artisan but the performance with it was terrible. Thats not the case with Artisan Pure for me. 6-8 hrs and decent projection. It's different to the original, but in the dry down I do get similar floral aspects.<br />
<br />
John Varvatos has some seriously underrated, beautiful fragrances in their lineup (John Varvatos, Vintage, Artisan, Artisan Pure).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1820637">SketchMotive</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-12">09/12/23 08:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is all about big rind-y, juicy citrus and green herbaceousness - you get all of that strong up front for about 30-60 minutes, but it dies down pretty quickly and unfortunately the base of this cologne is seriously lacking in power. I get a more basic (but nice) amber woodiness with light musk. Pleasant and smooth overall. This seems odd, but I also get a malty Fruit Loops note, but in a good way that blends nicely. Longevity is on the weak side of moderate at 3-4 hours total; it sits close after an hour or so. It's pretty nice if you don't need something too strong when the weather is on the warmer side, and I think it has an interesting enough character and the price is low enough to justify keeping around as an easy reach cheapie for summer.<br />
<br />
Almost forgot to mention... it has probably the worst atomizer I've ever seen - just comes out in a stream.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1926072"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1926072#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1915083" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Not there.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1863336"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1863336#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1862637" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1247086">razorsedge</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-23">06/23/23 01:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Great smelling summer frag if it wasn't for the abysmal performance.<br />
Citrusy and green in the opening, quickly turning soapy, and then completely gone in an hour. Must be  a JV thing because their other fragrance I've tried (Artisan Blu) also isn't a good performer. A shame really because it smells pretty good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1862637"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1862637#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1861278" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1861278" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Dylanturek"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1714268"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1714268.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Dylanturek" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Cobalt-Elixir-89374.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.89374.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bad Boy Cobalt Elixir"title="Bad Boy Cobalt Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1861278ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1861278" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1714268">Dylanturek</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-21">06/21/23 05:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was one of the first purchases I made a few years back when I decided I wanted more than one warm weather frag (YSL libre) and one cold weather frag (la Nuit de l'homme 2017). I don't consider myself a collector, but my shelf has grown since then and no matter how many niche or designer summer fragrances I love and wear, this one never gets boring or lets me down. If you don't like photorealistic citrus (this is a rindy orange the same way light blue forever is a rindy grapefruit), then you probably won't like this. If you like a more natural orange, as if you took the rind and expressed (twisted it) it over your skin the way you would finish a well crafted cocktail, then this will be a love. It is so uplifting and so calming, I can't help but reach for it in the morning when the weather is beautiful outside and I'm just feeling content with life (Zoloft helps). I get a very similar vibe from xerjoff mefisto even though they're completely different, they have the same uplifting and natural vibe to them. For the price, I'd rather try this first and see if you like it. If you do, I definitely suggest trying mefisto. Don't expect similar notes or a redundant smell: they are completely different. What you'll have are two incredibly natural and uplifting scents to accompany you and elevate your appreciation for summer. Forget performance, it doesn't matter. At this price and this quality/effect, overspray, respray and enjoy guilt-free. I get 4-6 hours, first two with moderate spillage, the rest more of a skin scent. I wear it for me and not impress anyone or attract attention, it just makes me happy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1861278"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1861278#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1860450" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1860450" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jgherrera"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1775049"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="jgherrera" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Lacoste-Fragrances/Eau-de-Lacoste-L-12-12-White-11043.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.11043.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Eau de Lacoste L.12.12. White"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1860450ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1860450" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1775049">jgherrera</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-20">06/20/23 04:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>In my case, it has a pungency which is highly disturbing to the nose. Like you're smelling a lemon that has gone putrid. It's not synthetic, but simply bitter/pungent beyond tolerance. When not in this 'aggressive' phase, there are moments when the perfume smells of an intensely sunny day in a citrus orchard.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1860450"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1860450#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1860006" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1860006" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Guccipordior"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1298002"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1298002.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Guccipordior" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Guerlain/L-Homme-Ideal-25780.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.25780.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="L’Homme Ideal"title="L’Homme Ideal"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1860006ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1860006" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1298002">Guccipordior</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-19">06/19/23 13:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a great summer fragrance that has become an easy dumb reach for me in the warm weather. Great citruses in the opening, the clementine is a nice sweet touch, it's super fresh and herbal. The petitgrain gives Artisan Pure that neroli vibe, but it's greener and earthier and not as floral as neroli. The whole fragrance is based around the citrus/petitgrain vibe and it dries down really nice to a woodier and muskier scent. The herbal and citrus facets of this are really nice and blend together very well. The musky drydown is really good and makes this a very good scent for the warm months that I don't think you'll catch many people wearing. It's not entirely unique, but it's different enough to warrant having if you are a fan of citrus/neroli/musky/woody scents. It's very mass appealing. Blind buy worthy unless you don't like neroli. The only Varvatos fragrance that I truly like. This one is actually a love for me. <br />
<br />
The bottle looks really cool. The atomizer isn't so great, but all you have to do is spray more. This is an affordable fragrance and worth getting the larger bottle of. There's no way you can overspray this because it's so fresh, clean, and herbal. Lasts a good amount of time. Expect around 5-6 hours before you'd have to reapply but the musky/woody drydown sticks around for a while. Fairly good projection and sillage too. You really can't go wrong with this one, in my opinion. Daytime scent, can even work for going out on a warm night.<br />
<br />
Anything with neroli will be compared to Neroli Portofino, it has that kinda vibe sure but its not as floral... it reminds me more of a woodier, muskier Banana Republic Neroli Woods, one of my favorite neroli based fragrances. Different enough but mass appealing enough to set itself apart from other neroli based fragrances.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1860006"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1860006#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1858031" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Not a serious fragrance tho, just something to wear when you’re going out in the sun doing your own relaxing thing. Not much of a compliment getter tbh…  more like “ You smell like lemons man, what is that?”. If you got the spare cash, or maybe you’re growing your collection… buy it. <br />
<br />

<br />
Edit: I’ve had the bottle for about 2 months now, and it’s my least favorite in my collection, I don’t reach for it as often because I gotta be in a specific mood to where this. <br />
<br />
Scent: 6/10<br />
Performance : 6/10<br />
Longevity : 8/10<br />
Compliments = Zero</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1852359"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1852359#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1852226" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1610271">Mojojojo85</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-26">04/26/23 20:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Since the first time I smelled it on a test strip I was in love with this one. The way the citrus notes shine in the opening is phenomenal. Not in your face citrus but very respectful almost earthy citrus. That starts to mix with the ginger and petitgrain in the middle to become a little earthy/herbal then dries down to a calming woodsy, musky base that blends well with the lingering citrus from the opening. It becomes quite linear after the opening but this is one of the few fragrances, IMO, where that works great for. Great for warmer months and even into early fall, day time and those spring and summer nights. Reminds me of Mexico. Just got my second bottle of this, surprisingly, at TJ MAXX for $45. Great fragrance to add to any collection, as it is very versatile and this is one of my all time favorites.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1818564"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1818564#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1816834" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I have just got back from a swim in the ocean, had a shower to wash off the saltwater, pulled on a pair of long white cotton pants, will go for a walk along the esplanade enjoying the sea breeze later this afternoon, and I’m wearing several sprays of Artisan Pure. <br />
<br />
The opening is incredible: on a level and similar to fragrances such as Xerjoff Nio, Dior Homme Cologne and Cedrat Enivrant. Bergamot and petitgrain are what I get most of in the opening. There is a mouth-watering sourness and bitterness at play, the olfactory equivalent of tasting some citrus zest rather than the pulp. <br />
<br />
The mid-notes are lightly herbal and cottony - think of pottering around the backyard wearing a cotton t-shirt with the fragrance of herbs wafting to you on a late afternoon breeze rather than burying your nose in them - and there is a hint of something almost balsamic in the drydown. Perfect for hot summer days near or at the beach, or if you’re wearing a casual linen shirt and pants, wearing a Panama hat and looking over your coffee/vanilla orchid/coca leaf plantation. Gorgeous bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1687213"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1687213#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1686289" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It does smell beautiful with such a smooth blend of citruses and florals. But this doesn't perform at all for me, becoming a skin scent maybe after an hour on a good day. JV fragrances are known for being weak performers but this is really disappointing. <br />
<br />
Again, the scent itself is gorgeous along with the bottle. But there are fragrances out there that smell very similar to this with a similar price point and much better longevity and projection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The petitgrain is far more prominent than those saying this is a citrus bomb would suggest. Quite herbal, only a bit powdery, but far more "white floral" than "citrus bomb". Great value if you can get it at pre-discontinued price. The Dior Homme Cologne comparison is there, but I prefer that, which is a true citrus bomb. DHC is like a sheer wall of lemonade citrus, this is like a happy cloud of citrusy white flowers. Dries down a bit bitter and more "clean white t shirt in an orange grove" where DHC is "juicy citrus relief in white t shirt weather". Beautiful bottle too. Recommend.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1645102"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1645102#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1643348" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Opens up with fresh, herbal citrus (I get more lemon and bergamot than orange and mandarin), quick dry-down after 20 mins becomes more pettigrain, small amount of ginger in the back. <br />
<br />
Edit: I wore this fragrance all day today in less heat (36-38 degs Celsius) and it’s become a skin scent after 6 hours with 7 sprays, which is a much better than previously (very high heat: 2 hours before becoming a skin scent). Sillage is average for a freshy and projection too. As a skin scent it is really good, some woods, orris root and some musk starting to come through. <br />
<br />
For the price, fresh scent and the unique look of the bottle, I would give it a 3.75/5. <br />
<br />
TL:DR: fresh citrus; longevity, sillage and projection average, decent price; safe blind-buy</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1637849"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1637849#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1628477" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
