padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1283300">Daviako</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-17">08/17/22 13:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There's one thing about this particular fragrance that's very unique...the bottle. This fragrance smells like the bottle it's in. White, crisp, clean, and powder-coated. Smelling this instantly takes me to being on a boat on a nice day with a slight breeze, wearing a loose white linen shirt, and just relaxing with a cocktail. While I do love this fragrance in its own right, it does come off right away as being very similar to 4711 Original, but if you give it a few moments, the differences begin to emerge. The citruses in the opening don't grab ahold of your nose as long as Artisan does, they fade quickly into the more herbal qualities of this flanker. The addition of the orris root gives it a much creamier dry down than Artisan as well. This is one of the few fragrances I'd say would work well in the hottest temperatures, at least it does for me in the sunshine state.<br />
<br />
9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1625605"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1625605#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1621724" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1621724" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="doodluv"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1386268"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1386268.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="doodluv" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Ormonde-Jayne/4-Montabaco-Intensivo-67775.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.67775.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="4. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/869924">Abdulrehman Maqsood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-07-27">07/27/22 20:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Got a sampler, here are my thoughts:<br />
Starts off smelling very herbaceous and sweet citrus-like. Think Terre d'heremes if you've ever smelled it but more heavy on the zest and less amber-y. <br />
<br />
15 minutes later: The delicious citrus is still the main note here, which I like very much! It has ever so slightly mellowed and the herbs have taken a slight step forward-so to speak. Its pretty linear till now but I absolutely love it as it is.<br />
<br />
The mellow down: Oh my god this is amazing. The citrus has mellowed quite a bit but its still definitely the most prominent note here, the lovely sweet tang is still the first thing i notice with each whiff. Added to that; a cooling touch of white musk and some woody notes truly round this fragrance up into masterpiece levels for me.<br />
<br />
This was a very pleasant surprise! This is probably one of the most beautiful 'uplifting/fresh' category fragrances i've smelled since I've stated sampling them. It is definitely in my To-buy list for the future.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1611914"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1611914#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1606006" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Than this beautiful citrus herbal frag shines! 🍋🍋🍋🍋🍋.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1606006"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1606006#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1598858" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1598858" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RileyB"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/862747"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.862747.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RileyB" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Comme-des-Garcons/Comme-des-Garcons-Series-4-Cologne-Anbar-3634.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.3634.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Comme des Garcons Series 4 Cologne : Anbar"title="Comme des Garcons Series 4 Cologne : Anbar"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1598858ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1598858" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/862747">RileyB</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-07-07">07/07/22 23:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I find these JV Artisan bottles intriguing. Makes me wonder what gadget gets used to wind the outer in such an ordered yet unordered fashion. Very fitting for the product line though, ‘artisan’. <br />
Anyway, aesthetics aside, more importantly whats in the bottle.<br />
For me the top is absolutely my favourite part. The citrus notes really do give the effect of a white floral in the direction of neroli or orange blossom. That’s backed by a subtle herbal undercurrent that definitely leans this in the masculine direction. The use of the word ‘Pure’ in that regard is very apt. It’s a very clean, almost translucent white floral citrus. <br />
However - typically with so many JV scents - the top rapidly descends into a different heart where within about 15 to 20 mins the petitgrain mixed with the remaining subtle nuances of thyme and marjoram rapidly overtakes the citrus to convert the scent into a very powdery herbal type aroma that continues for the full extent of the dry down. Petitgrain being at the fore front of that delivery, with the orris and musk adding a large dose of powder. I get little to no ginger interestingly enough. Nor a great deal of woods either. Mainly just a very powdery herbal petitgrain type aroma.<br />
Do I like how it smells, yes! Its certainly has its own character and quite a refined smell, but I do pine for the top notes to last longer, they really are divine.<br />
These things said, here’s where JVAP shines for me; I love white florals - but only if there’s something in the scent that leans it enough in a masculine direction to be wearable for a guy. For that reason, this is an excellent base for layering under white floral scents that might be considered ‘unisex’ but lean in a more feminine direction. The petitgrain herbal aspect immediately adds a more masculine foundation that reorients what’s being layered on top if it to be more masculine. Further more it seems to have the capacity to extend the life of the floral being layered on it. Perfect!<br />
So this is a love for me,  but not for the reasons one might assume. So much so that I have a backup bottle for layering because its so versatile and fit for that purpose.<br />
These things said, for those wanting it as just a straight scent, its best for summer to help extend the life of the very appealing citrus top.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; But those notes go away quickly, and leave a longer, drier accord of petitgrain and ginger. Overall this wears as a fairly dry citrus aromatic: petitgrain (the scent of a young orange tree leaf) lasts longer than many other citrus notes, but it's also quite a bit more arid than the smells of citrus fruit juices. <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1517421">ishootlikeaking</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-06-30">06/30/22 13:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Blind bought this and kind of regretted it a little bit, first spray it’s very citrusy but after an hour or so it turns woody and gingery. More than anything, the amount you put on yourself is what will determine what it comes out to smelling like. I find that if i spray too much, the herbal, fresh garden, almost fresh veggies comes out. When i spray a little and keep it light, the lemon shines and it is so citrusy. It doesn’t last very long like all the other comments have said but unfortunately citrusy fragrances tend to be weaker than other fragrances. I definitely compare this one to ck1, except artisan pure would be a darker more mature version. I don’t like Artisan Pure by itself BUT layering it with st barts by tommy bahama actually makes it smell so much better and makes it last a tiny bit longer.  I wouldn’t pay full price for a bottle of this but I would pick this up if it were at a discount store (which is what i did). The bottle is definitely pretty though so if you care more about the bottle and not so much the fragrance then 10/10 recommend. All in all if you’re looking to buy a John Varvatos Fragrance then the best one would be John Varvatos by John Varvatos because of its uniqueness where I feel like Artisan Pure is a little basic.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
In short: smells great, just wish it had more oomph.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1582525"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1582525#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1572097" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1572097" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ZeroLeon"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1286218"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ZeroLeon" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1572097ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1572097" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1508991">alexxf35</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-25">05/25/22 05:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>One of my favorite summer scents.  Be very careful though as this is much more complex and less mass appealing than the typical fresh/citrus blue fragrance.<br />
<br />
Huge amounts of orange and citrus on the opening.  Not as sweet as you would think, but more of a dank, almost fermented/bitter feel.  The petitgrain comes out quickly in the mid, which gives this a far different, more grown up take than most.<br />
<br />
Dries down nicely and for me lasts surprisingly long.  Awesome t-shirt and shorts cologne for summer, but don't expect a ton of sweet or freshness in this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1570761"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1570761#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1568687" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
No no, this stuff is decent AND great. AND better than other similar options within the price range. <br />
<br />
With this you get an explosion of 4 zingy bright citruses, ginger, herbs, and light musk. This stuff is just mind blowing for summer. My very first thought was it reminded me of sparkling champagne. It's somewhere between chill and casual and energetic and playful. This is like 12pm noon in July when the sun is the most intense.<br />
<br />
Not only is this a unique citrus but the herbs musk and woods make this rather long lasting for a citrus cologne. Hands down one of John Varvatos best fragrances and possibly one of the best bottles in the designer fragrance realm.<br />
<br />
If you are a fan of fragrances along the likes of Tommy for men, Chanel AH Blanche, D&amp;G PH, Invictus Aqua 16, &amp; YSL Y Eau Fraiche this ones for you! Artisan Pure is within this family without cloning ANY of them and doing its own thing despite phonepotatos claims. You will NOT have another fragrance that smells like this. Unless you have the original Artisan or something which isn't even as good as Artisan Pure. <br />
<br />
Summer masterpiece that will always be in my collection. <br />
<br />
10 10 10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1564083"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1564083#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1563111" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1563111" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="PhonePotato"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1224212"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1224212.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="PhonePotato" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Aaron-Terence-Hughes/Supernova-90884.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.90884.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Supernova"title="Supernova"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1563111ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1563111" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1224212">PhonePotato</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-13">05/13/22 11:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It’s decent, but not great… actually it’s not even good when you compare it to all the other similar options within the price range. <br />
<br />
That being said if you can get a tester for $30 then I’d say it’s worth it if you don't have anything else similar in your collection. That’s the big problem though,you probably already have a few frags that smell just like this.<br />
<br />
There’s just nothing that makes this stand out.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1563111"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1563111#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1558615" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1558615" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheSuperSniffer"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1363621"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1363621.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheSuperSniffer" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Pineward-Perfumes/Murkwood-64600.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.64600.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Murkwood"title="Murkwood"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1558615ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1558615" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1363621">TheSuperSniffer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-06">05/06/22 17:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not sure why I never reviewed this one. I've had my bottle for two years - sold one, and bought another. Here we go. <br />
<br />
Citrus-based fragrances are difficult to stand out as "unique", therefore, they're often ignored or lumped into one vague, generic category. The "reminds me of" list here is downright perplexing, and I'll explain that soon, but first, the perfume. <br />
<br />
Artisan Pure opens up incredibly bright, crisp, airy, and fresh, with petitgrain being the obvious centre. Imaging pulling the leaves from a lemon tree, and gently breaking them in your hands - fresh, bright, aromatic, citrus, but not juicy, and fairly green. This green, herbal, aromatic petitgrain is complimented by a subtle touch of fresh thyme. Fuzzy, aromatic and green, but not at all savoury. Alongside this green, herbal opening, is an almost equal presence of bergamot. The bergamot is incredibly soft (in texture, not presence), bright, and almost juicy, while lending a bit of perceived sweetness to what would otherwise be bone dry. Beneath the green and citrusy foundation of petitgrain and bergamot, a unique juicy citrus facet emerges, and that would be either mandarin or clementine. A sweet, luscious, juicy Satsuma mandarin wedge, and it really is what lends the complex twist to an otherwise typical citrus composition. In this opening-mid phase, you have a fresh, bright, and rather interesting combination of green and citrus, which introduces just enough sweetness to make it feel ultra-modern, but still remain timeless, and not overtly synthetic. <br />
<br />
As we move into the heart of the fragrance, the fresh green character of petitgrain and thyme burn off a bit, bringing soft oily bergamot to the forefront, with the mandarin trailing behind. There's a soft white floral wisp peeking through, but it doesn't scream neroli. In fact, there's really little-to-no neroli character here, which is why I cannot say it is accurate to compare this to Neroli Portofino, 4711, Wood Neroli, Canvas, or any of those perfumes. The neroli just isn't here to draw similarities. To my nose, it also shies away from lemon avoiding any floor cleaner associations. There's no real "orange" character, like in JV Artisan (which to my nose, was pure orange-scented disinfectant), and Artisan Pure couldn't be more different from Artisan. A bit of ambroxan, clean modern musks, and a kiss of woody warmth begin to rise from the base, adding some bottom end, but always keeping the bright citrusy freshness at the heart. As it wears on, it softens, and it takes on a fluffy, almost "powdery" softness, which, to my nose, doesn't translate as iris or orris, but it's very pleasing and inviting, contrasting the bright, bracing zest from the top. Ultimately, a sort of soft, semi-sweet, semi-floral, semi-citrus sort of lemongrass note forms, and enters the mix as part of the base. Throughout the wear, the bergamot remains the star player, with the fragrant citrus element of petitgrain overtaking the green element, soft mandarin zest, lemongrass, that fluffy softness, a warm kiss of amber, and just a whisper of herbal greenness all following behind, until it ultimately settles to a skin scent and fades. <br />
<br />
I actually get pretty fair longevity out of this one, especially considering it being a citrus perfume. The bombastic nature of the opening settles fairly quickly, and will project well out past an arm's length for a couple of hours, before enveloping you in a personal scent bubble for another several. On average, I get about 5 hours of "performance" from this, before it stays on the skin. The atomizer on these JV bottles - while producing a fine, wide mist, barely gives you anything. It's but a little puff of a spray. Much like a little lipstick atomizer, if not even less. You have to "overspray" to get what you'd get from a typical bottle with a better atomizer. A Dior spray would equate to about 6 of these sprays. Otherwise, longevity is perfectly fine. <br />
<br />
All-in-all, the fact that I cannot think of a single perfume that this reminds me of, in a sea of citrus perfumes of varying lineage, actually makes Artisan Pure rather unique in that regard, with its interesting bergamot-mandarin-petitgrain top, and soft, fluffy heart. It's absolutely stunning in ultra high heat, and never becomes cloying. It's clean, fresh, and extremely pleasing - will never offend those around you. Paired with some white linen pants and a tight white button-down or tee, this one could garner positive attention. I think it has a place in any collection, and it does exactly what it intends to, and it does it brilliantly. And for the price is typically goes for, I think it's a summer staple, and a pretty safe blind buy, if you enjoy bergamot or petitgrain and want a unique twist on it. It's just difficult not to enjoy this one, and I look forward to breaking it out again, with the warmer weather fast approaching. <br />
<br />
Wear it to the beach on a warm day, or on a nature walk in the sun, or just to a fancy restaurant for lunch, dressed in something you feel confident in, and I think it'll click into place for you. <br />
<br />
Scent: 7.5/10<br />
Longevity: 6.5/10<br />
Projection: 7/10<br />
Uniqueness: 7/10<br />
Value: 8.5/10<br />
Atomizer: 3/10<br />
Mass likeability: 9/10<br />
Blind buy safe: Yes, if you like bergamot/citrus<br />
<br />
Overall: 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1558615"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1558615#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1558602" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="strike-title"><span>Most Popular Positive Reviews</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent1833907" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1833907" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Br&#039;eauDeCologne"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/857045"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.857045.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Br&#039;eauDeCologne" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1833907ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1833907" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/857045">Br&#039;eauDeCologne</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-15">05/15/23 16:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A sparkling gem of a fragrance that stands out from the crowd.  No calone.  No ambroxan. Just a smooth, herbal citrus masterpiece of a scent; the quality of which seems like thrice its price, especially against some of the so-called "niche" offerings these days.  <br />
<br />
Suitable for any occasion, from a quiet evening at home with friends to a formal night out on the town.  Classy, yet not presumptuous.  Refined, yet not stuffy.  <br />
<br />
Brilliant in its accessibility and being easy to wear, Artisan Pure is in a class of one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1833907"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1833907#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1461735" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1461735" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Seuni"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1266523"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1266523.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Seuni" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1461735ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1461735" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1266523">Seuni</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-12-11">12/11/21 15:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So. Time to bust some myths.<br />
<br />
1. It's not linear. It starts very green - bergamot based marjojram and thyme is very apparent and on my skin are gone in 15-30 in minutes. Tle citrus/clementine Vibe stays for another 3 hours tops, then it becomes fresh, musky, woodsy masculine skin scent.<br />
<br />
2. It's not that bad with performance - it's the sprayer that is shit. It produces like a tiny turberculoid man breath each time you spray, almost no juice - that's why people don't get performance. For a citrus it's completely normal. It's a shit sprayer edt, use more juice people.<br />
<br />
I'm both positively and negatively surprised about the quality. The collar of the sprayer has the name of the fragrance facing to the side, it's not centered. It's very crooked. The sprayer is shit - distribution is nice, just tiny. You need to spray a lot. The cap is wooden - which is nice, it's just it's the lightest wood I ever had between my fingers. It's lighter than plastic. It slides on, no click, it's friction-based.<br />
But the design is nice overall, and the 'basket' thing is natural, not plastic, the bottle is frosted.<br />
<br />
Repair the sprayer, center the collar and make a better cap - otherwise it's a very nice citrus scent. Summer, heat, daytime. 5-7 (depending on skin chemistry, sweating and temperature).<br />
<br />
@edit - I centered the collar myself 🙃</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1461735"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1461735#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent905924" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/846250">picknenders</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-01-29">01/29/18 18:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I can see why people say “this reminds me of (insert citrus)...”<br />
<br />
It is familiar - and I do believe that it is the least unique of the artisan line. <br />
<br />
This, however, is where my criticism stops. As with literally every single other varvatos smell, this is pleasing, smooth and refined. I like that this has a bitter/earthy vibe hiding beneath the top. This is a tad less bright than Lalique white/Parfums de Marly Galloway - but I find them similar. The aforementioned frgrances both contain tamarind- which plays really well with citrus - giving it (to me) an earthy/bitter nuance. I find that varvatos pure also produces the same result, but I don’t see tamarind listed. Not sure where it’s coming from, but it’s there. Regardless, this is yet another great addition to the already-stacked varvatos collection. <br />
<br />
Side note - if varvatos could release a dark-fruity-amber, an animalic and maybe a fourgere, I’d happily get rid of my entire collection and just rock JV scents.<br />
<br />
7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="905924"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=905924#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent863386" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc863386" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Calvini"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/518579"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.518579.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Calvini" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma863386ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd863386" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/518579">Calvini</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-09-21">09/21/17 20:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is easily the best citrus based Varvatos—smells natural, no aquatic note, and none of that "popular male cologne" vibe, instead very unisex and genuine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="863386"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=863386#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1558615" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1558615" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheSuperSniffer"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1363621"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1363621.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheSuperSniffer" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Pineward-Perfumes/Murkwood-64600.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.64600.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Murkwood"title="Murkwood"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1558615ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1558615" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1363621">TheSuperSniffer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-05-06">05/06/22 17:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not sure why I never reviewed this one. I've had my bottle for two years - sold one, and bought another. Here we go. <br />
<br />
Citrus-based fragrances are difficult to stand out as "unique", therefore, they're often ignored or lumped into one vague, generic category. The "reminds me of" list here is downright perplexing, and I'll explain that soon, but first, the perfume. <br />
<br />
Artisan Pure opens up incredibly bright, crisp, airy, and fresh, with petitgrain being the obvious centre. Imaging pulling the leaves from a lemon tree, and gently breaking them in your hands - fresh, bright, aromatic, citrus, but not juicy, and fairly green. This green, herbal, aromatic petitgrain is complimented by a subtle touch of fresh thyme. Fuzzy, aromatic and green, but not at all savoury. Alongside this green, herbal opening, is an almost equal presence of bergamot. The bergamot is incredibly soft (in texture, not presence), bright, and almost juicy, while lending a bit of perceived sweetness to what would otherwise be bone dry. Beneath the green and citrusy foundation of petitgrain and bergamot, a unique juicy citrus facet emerges, and that would be either mandarin or clementine. A sweet, luscious, juicy Satsuma mandarin wedge, and it really is what lends the complex twist to an otherwise typical citrus composition. In this opening-mid phase, you have a fresh, bright, and rather interesting combination of green and citrus, which introduces just enough sweetness to make it feel ultra-modern, but still remain timeless, and not overtly synthetic. <br />
<br />
As we move into the heart of the fragrance, the fresh green character of petitgrain and thyme burn off a bit, bringing soft oily bergamot to the forefront, with the mandarin trailing behind. There's a soft white floral wisp peeking through, but it doesn't scream neroli. In fact, there's really little-to-no neroli character here, which is why I cannot say it is accurate to compare this to Neroli Portofino, 4711, Wood Neroli, Canvas, or any of those perfumes. The neroli just isn't here to draw similarities. To my nose, it also shies away from lemon avoiding any floor cleaner associations. There's no real "orange" character, like in JV Artisan (which to my nose, was pure orange-scented disinfectant), and Artisan Pure couldn't be more different from Artisan. A bit of ambroxan, clean modern musks, and a kiss of woody warmth begin to rise from the base, adding some bottom end, but always keeping the bright citrusy freshness at the heart. As it wears on, it softens, and it takes on a fluffy, almost "powdery" softness, which, to my nose, doesn't translate as iris or orris, but it's very pleasing and inviting, contrasting the bright, bracing zest from the top. Ultimately, a sort of soft, semi-sweet, semi-floral, semi-citrus sort of lemongrass note forms, and enters the mix as part of the base. Throughout the wear, the bergamot remains the star player, with the fragrant citrus element of petitgrain overtaking the green element, soft mandarin zest, lemongrass, that fluffy softness, a warm kiss of amber, and just a whisper of herbal greenness all following behind, until it ultimately settles to a skin scent and fades. <br />
<br />
I actually get pretty fair longevity out of this one, especially considering it being a citrus perfume. The bombastic nature of the opening settles fairly quickly, and will project well out past an arm's length for a couple of hours, before enveloping you in a personal scent bubble for another several. On average, I get about 5 hours of "performance" from this, before it stays on the skin. The atomizer on these JV bottles - while producing a fine, wide mist, barely gives you anything. It's but a little puff of a spray. Much like a little lipstick atomizer, if not even less. You have to "overspray" to get what you'd get from a typical bottle with a better atomizer. A Dior spray would equate to about 6 of these sprays. Otherwise, longevity is perfectly fine. <br />
<br />
All-in-all, the fact that I cannot think of a single perfume that this reminds me of, in a sea of citrus perfumes of varying lineage, actually makes Artisan Pure rather unique in that regard, with its interesting bergamot-mandarin-petitgrain top, and soft, fluffy heart. It's absolutely stunning in ultra high heat, and never becomes cloying. It's clean, fresh, and extremely pleasing - will never offend those around you. Paired with some white linen pants and a tight white button-down or tee, this one could garner positive attention. I think it has a place in any collection, and it does exactly what it intends to, and it does it brilliantly. And for the price is typically goes for, I think it's a summer staple, and a pretty safe blind buy, if you enjoy bergamot or petitgrain and want a unique twist on it. It's just difficult not to enjoy this one, and I look forward to breaking it out again, with the warmer weather fast approaching. <br />
<br />
Wear it to the beach on a warm day, or on a nature walk in the sun, or just to a fancy restaurant for lunch, dressed in something you feel confident in, and I think it'll click into place for you. <br />
<br />
Scent: 7.5/10<br />
Longevity: 6.5/10<br />
Projection: 7/10<br />
Uniqueness: 7/10<br />
Value: 8.5/10<br />
Atomizer: 3/10<br />
Mass likeability: 9/10<br />
Blind buy safe: Yes, if you like bergamot/citrus<br />
<br />
Overall: 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="46623"comment_id="1558615"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/John-Varvatos/Artisan-Pure-46623.html?ccid=1558615#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="46623" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
